v-pre><p><b>Aventus</b> by <b>Creed</b> is a Chypre Fruity fragrance for men. <b>Aventus</b> was launched in 2010. Aventus was created by Jean-Christophe Hérault and Erwin Creed. Top notes are Bergamot, Black Currant, Apple, Lemon and Pink Pepper; middle notes are Pineapple, Patchouli and Moroccan Jasmine; base notes are Birch, Musk, oak moss, Ambroxan and Cedarwood. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Aventus celebrates strength, vision and success, inspired by the dramatic life of war, peace and romance lived by Emperor Napoleon. The bottle is emblazoned with a silver emblem of a horse and rider.</p>

<p>The finest ingredients were hand-selected for this composition, and father and son developed this provocative, masculine and optimistic fragrance as a joint effort.</p>

<p>Top notes: blackcurrant, bergamot, apple and pineapple. Heart: rose, dry birch, Moroccan jasmine and patchouli. Base: oak moss, musk, ambergris, and vanilla.</p>

<p>Aventus is available in flacons of 30, 75, 120 and 250 ml.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541">ALakota</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 17:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Awhatvus? Psh. 1 spray terre de hermes, 1 spray salt &amp; pepper, 1 spray elysium parfum, 2 sprays elysium cologne, 2 sprays blue agave. Now we're a lemon, bros 🍋 a dirty lemon from heaven 😌 If you like aventus and top-notch chypre fragrances, definitely give elysium a look. I think it's the best after a ludicrous amount of buying aventus imitators from small houses, club de nuit of every sort obviously, a few different eras &amp; batches of aventus, etc. etc. Get a decant of elysium and see what you think, and try the new aventus if you can get a good price. I hear it's decent. But don't waste your life hunting down primo batches of aventus and paying your soul, because odds are club de nuit parfum limited is probably better, and Elysium is DEFINITELY better, especially the parfum. Aventus is still unique enough for what it is regardless of batch, and was innovative for its time so what the hell 10/10. After smelling all of these side by side, right now, I still gotta say that my L4221X01E batches (last 2 bottles I have and probably nothing special) probably beat everything else if I'm being honest. Just my opinion. The best Aventus clones I ever tried were probably Scentual Obsessions King of Kings, King Fragrances Monarch, and Pineapple Intense from Montagne in that order, first to last, but Monarch and King of Kings are really close. Pineapple vintage intense from Parfums Vintage was also amazing and got me a lot of compliments <br />
a few years ago. Club de Nuit Intense Man Limited Parfum is probably the best fragrance out of any of these besides Elysium depending on your taste, but I don't look at that as an Aventus "clone" the way most people do, saying it is identical. It is nowhere even CLOSE to identical, but they are both top-notch. All the club de nuit intense man are pretty great though. I don't know what the market is like nowadays, but don't fuss too much over version if it's gonna cost you your legs. If you're going to spend your legs, get Elysium cologne and parfum and save money in the end in this endless quest. They're just too damn good in their ingredients and composition and can't be beat in this realm.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2320224"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2320224#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85); padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2317864" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Hieu Do"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2288954"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Hieu Do" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2317864ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2317864" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2288954">Hieu Do</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-16">10/16/24 13:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have never commented on this forum, but today I had to register and comment. I EXTREMELY agree with @Robusto's comment below.<br />
<br />
I have been using Aventus since 2019 and it is my signature scent and use it almost every day. I am an actual perfume user, not a collector, which means that any scent I buy MUST be used, not for display. So in all 4 seasons of the year, I use about 4 scents in rotation, and am extremely strict so that they suit my skin and my nose.<br />
<br />
Going back to Aventus, because this is actually the scent I absolutely love, not only because it suits my nose but also makes me a lot more confident in life and work, as well as receiving a lot of compliments from everyone. Man, these are real compliments! Before writing more, I want to say that if you have used Aventus (not the crazy fan who collects 1000 batches), you must admit that there are differences between batches. Now, the reason I wrote that I strongly agree with @Robusto's comment below is because my bottle of F batches just happened to be the same F001750, and it REALLY REALLY made me think of the first bottle of Aventus as 17Y02, code bottle that makes me fall in love with this scent. This batch F001750 is so so good.<br />
<br />
I need to say a little more, you can say ''OK so that's good, what's so crazy about it?'' That's because I know the smell of Aventus has changed, because after using up 17Y02, I bought a new bottle with the mindset of ''Let's move on to whatever's new'', that's 19Y01N (Of course while using this new bottle I also let it age and bought older and even newer batch bottles to experiment with, so trust me I know how this scent has changed, and the superpower of old batches). OMFG, it really smells much fresher, even though it's still super delicious, but to my nose it's harsh, not The scent 100% captivated me like 17Y02. And now with this F batches, Creed has somewhat returned and done things properly when in Kering's hands. BUT, this new F batch also has this and that. If you did a google search, you'll see new F batch bottles with a metal cap and no black lettering in common. However, notice that there are brand new box with black stamps with gold numberals (like my F001750, F002090,...) and white stamps like F001925,.... The important thing is that I tried the decant of genuine F001925 and it smells like Club de nuit, it's very dark and doesn't show any freshness, which I don't understand why, if you don't believe it you can find decant and try it, it doesn't smell luxurious and elegant at all. The last thing that surprised me was that I had just told the store where I bought all the real perfume bottles, also where I bought F001750, I didn't tell them what color stamp the F001925 bottle was.<br />
<br />
And you know what they told me? They immediately said "we really don't know what Creed's intention is that they make the scent of the bottles with gold numbers and black stamps better than the bottles packaged with white stamps". This proves that the sellers knew right from the beginning which types of packaging have the ability to smell better, and more luxurious. After all, my advice is to look for new F batch bottles (if you don't want to be lost in the hunt for old batches with high risk rates like 15-16-17-18-19), but with black stamps and gold numbers (like the image of my bottle F001750, you can find it on google). Thanks for reading.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2317864"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2317864#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2317679" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2313954" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="austinmdpedi"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2073655"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2073655.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="austinmdpedi" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2313954ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2313954" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2073655">austinmdpedi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-12">10/12/24 22:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It was 2014. I found myself divorced. Time for a life makeover and after 20+ years scentless, one of my choices was to buy a “cologne.”  I read an Esquire article and bought Aventus. It felt intimidating to wear… it was so “strong.” The compliments came quickly though. It was a nice confidence boost. A great step in my journey. It was my only fragrance for five or so years.  Ten years later, I have a different perspective. Fragrance doesn’t make “the man.”  Confidence allows me to wear what I want, and I’m primarily now wearing fragrance for me. Yet, I’ll always be grateful for this scent. It holds a special place for me and though I rarely wear it now, I’ll always own a bottle. <br />
<br />
To me, it is a great all-arounder. If you had to only own one fragrance you could do far worse than to choose this. It is a good office scent but can get out of hand if over applied. I’ve always gotten 8-10 hours from it as well. <br />
<br />
It is well described in the endless reviews. Bright. Citrus. Floral. Ginger. A bit of an attractive acrid bite. Dry down is epic. Woody and musky. <br />
<br />
Beware that a lot of the reviews here appear to be off cheap clones. <br />
<br />
Price and value are always relative. If you don’t want to spend this much, buy something else. So much whining here. A little (2-3 sprays) goes a long way. Can be found well discounted at reliable sellers as well.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2313954"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2313954#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2312132" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; At first, quite fresh and citrusy with a hint of blackcurrant. I do detect some faint smoke and wet wood (possibly moss?). I expected it to have a very strong and explicit pineapple scent, but it doesn't. I get some pineapple but it is very faint and nicely blends in with all the other elements. As time passes, it gets a bit sweeter, but still remains fresh. I think it is nicely blended and does smell good, but in a very generic male fragrance way. I think this could be a nice allrounder, that you can wear anytime, but it isn't "OMG HOW AMAZING" in any situation. The sillage is quite weak, I have to get quite close to smell it. Overall it is good, but I am not sure the hype or the price is justified.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2311829"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2311829#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2311749" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; After 2019, the quality went downhill and could not justify spending this much money on something that was a shell of its former self. I was skeptical about buying a new bottle but Aventus has a spot near and dear to my heart and couldn't resist. I have it a few full wearings and was surprised with how much projection and longevity I was getting. I put the bottle away for a few months and WOW did it change!! Everything feels like it ramped up and was getting the same vibes I used to get from my 2015-2017 bottles! No, they are not the same as my older batches in regards to the depth....they are the same with how much projection and longevity I used to get. There is this dank vanilla/musk and ash (not smoke) in the dry down that hits me like what Aventus used to do. Thank you Creed for bringing Aventus back to respectability. BTW, my new bottle is batch F1750.<br />

The most beautiful men's fragrance I've smelled so far. There is majestic old school like Fahrenheit, Obession, Cool Water, then there is a transition - Declaration, L'eau par Kenzo, Boss Bottled and then there are last days sweet-boyish Invictus/Eros etc. that dominate the market. There are of course examples like Sauvage, Bleu de Chanel that update this fresh old school vibe. <br />
<br />
This too has bits from the old school and bits from what is considered modern. <br />
<br />
Scent profile? See it for yourself. It has many impeccable clones. You try it once, you won't forget it.<br />
<br />
Performance is good, but actually could have been better, especially sillage.<br />
<br />
Price? I think these 200$ tags are just stupid and bourgeois and make me feel a communist. This one should be the proletariat perfume for all</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2303225"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2303225#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2302899" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Aventus cologne is way better than this is or ever was.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2302899"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2302899#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2302330" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2302330" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Nick-Euphonia"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2271678"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2271678.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Nick-Euphonia" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2302330ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2302330" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2271678">Nick-Euphonia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-02">10/02/24 08:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a very recent batch that I'm reviewing. Never really smelled the older batches, but I mean, if the older batches smelled (and obviously, performed) any better than this; than this fragrance deserved all the hype (for those older batches). The scent is bright, citrus, pineapple, smooth as silk, perfectly balanced, clean and gorgeous. A well structured, wonderfully put-together fragrance. It's obvious the ingredients are high quality, there is no harshness, bite or offensive note to be found from start to finish. BUT - good Lord, the price and the performance. I tested this on a strip, and found the scent faded fairly fast. Which is really telling, considering scents can easily last on a strip for days. When I wore it, I put on the better part of a 2ml sampler, and people said they could not smell it. And people even commented "You should probably wear something else, because I can't smell it." It became a skin scent within probably an hour. And I have quite oily skin and such things are not really a problem for me.<br />
<br />
I tested this and Mont Blanc Explorer on strips together and after the top notes died off, I honestly thought the Explorer was more pleasant to smell, just because it was so much stronger and left a better impression. Even within an hour, it was as if the Aventus had been dried down to the faintest smell. Like listening to a song you love, but you can barely hear it at all.<br />
<br />
Fantastic scent, really a true 10/10 for the scent alone, but for the performance, no one can justify the price. 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2302330"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2302330#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2299695" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2296863" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Limboroom"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2230535"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Limboroom" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2296863ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2296863" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2230535">Limboroom</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-27">09/27/24 08:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A few months ago, I picked up Aventus and the 2 major clones, CDNIM (EPD, EDT), L’Aventure.  I was very curious about all of these differentially, not in a vacuum, so I will group them together to chat about.<br />
<br />
First, I would recommend them all.  TBH - the clones are so cheap, if you like citrus and smoke, it’s doesn’t make sense not to get them.  They all smell great.  And the performance is pretty good - my wife can smell them all on me for hours after application.  If I apply in the morning, I can still smell on my skin at bedtime.<br />
<br />
Plus, all 3 really are in the same family.  I’d say in general they are around 80-90% similar.  But that 10% difference is significant.<br />
<br />
CDNIM - EDT and EDP are like 95% the same.  And the differences are not enough to be super significant.  Yes, the openings, but that only lasts a few minutes.  The actual scent is a crisp just cut lemon pepper and some smoke.  <br />
<br />
L’Aventure - sweeter than CDNIM.  This is more fruity lemonade than the natural lemon from CDNIM.  Similar smoke, but a bit less pepper than CDNIM.  More similar to Aventus because of that less pepper and more sweetness.<br />
<br />
Aventus - the hype is real.  There is a roundness and a dimension that the smokey pineapple adds that you just don’t get in the clones.  You just really, really need to try it.  I only have F batches, 2 different ones, but both perform pretty well.  For as great as it is, in no way is this, or any fragrance worth the MSRP.  Anything over $300 doesn’t make a lot of sense.  But for the discounter’s, like a Jomashop, on sale price of less than $250, or sometimes Costco at around $200…IMO, this is worth it.  It is that good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2296863"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2296863#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2293201" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2291213" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Glue"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1896091"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1896091.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Glue" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Amouage/Boundless-66528.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.66528.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Boundless"title="Boundless"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2291213ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2291213" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1896091">Glue</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-22">09/22/24 04:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It's high quality and smells really decent but it's way too overhyped nowadays. I can imagine it was amazing when it came out but there are so many clones out there that it's nothing special anymore and simply not worth the price.<br />
I did want to buy it as I have CDNI and Cedrait Boise and enjoy both. Compared it on my skin next to CDNI Parfum and while the opening is much better, after 30min it's virtually the same scent. The only difference is that CDNI lasts whole day, while Aventus lasted maybe 2 hours on my skin with very little projection.<br />
<br />
I really wouldn't recommend it unless you have the money and owning the original somehow makes you feel better. For me it just wasn't worth it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2291213"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2291213#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2291109" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2283725" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Casiquire"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/942733"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Casiquire" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2283725ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2283725" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/942733">Casiquire</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-15">09/15/24 11:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Aventus is a loud explosion of citrus, bit of pineapple, and some smoky woody patchouli. It smells fantastic and masculine despite the "fruitiness". It is not too sweet or cloying whatsoever but it is bright and piercing, and it has the "wow" factor which gets compliments. It lasts for days on clothes (not quite as long on skin but still great) and projects like a monster. I got complimented in a smoky club just from one single spray, and someone fifteen feet away turned around and chimed in, so reviews talking about using seven sprays...y'all we can smell you across the whole continent, tone it down!<br />
<br />
There's a lot of bad information about this smell out there. It is extremely potent and long-lasting but it quickly turns you nose-blind. That's why you see mentions of poor performance. Please don't reapply this two hours later. Ambroxan lingers on clothes and skin for days, that's an objective fact. But the more you wear this the less you smell it. Go easy on the trigger and just trust the fragrance. One or two sprays is enough especially for indoors. Maybe you'll find it's a better value than you thought. <br />
<br />
The other big controversy with this scent is the variation. Batch variations are very real, but also very overblown. I still have bottles from 2013, 2015, etc and can easily compare side by side. There are subtle differences between bottles but it's overwhelmingly the same scent. It's true, my oldest bottles are slightly smokier and darker. However only half of that difference is because of batch variations or reformulations. Much of the difference is just the fact that the bottle had a decade to age. My nose tells me there's also been a change in the oakmoss, and I know that's a heavily regulated ingredient. Again, it's subtle. <br />
<br />
Just relax and, again, trust the scent. It didn't get this big for no reason.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2283725"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2283725#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2282802" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Scent: 10/10 (certain batches)<br />
Performance: 5/10 ( Skin scent after the 3rd hour)<br />
Projection: 4/10 (unless you do 20 sprays)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2278514"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2278514#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2278487" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Stop caring about the longevity of this fragrance.<br />
<br />
This EASILY lasts all day (10hrs+). You do not want ANY Creed fragrance to smell like an extrait, you need to understand the philosophy of Creed is not the mainstream idea of maximum performance and maximum longevity but deriving of many facets of natural materials that make this fragrance create an AURA of scent, and no other house I've tried creates this so perfectly, not even the dozen mainstream clones can recreate the way this fragrance is built. It is so well done, inoffensive, clean, projects a bubble, can pick whiffs up throughout the entire afternoon.<br />
<br />
Go up to somebody on the 10th hour, they will tell you that they smell Aventus.<br />
<br />
Oh, and yes, if you are wondering - this is a 2023 batch of review. I have owned many others that have that Aura scent bubble.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2276351"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2276351#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276062" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2040463">Pick</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-05">09/05/24 06:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Truly a beautiful scent that I believe to be extremely over-hated, going from one of the best colognes on earth just a few years ago to being "overrated" "overhyped" and "smelling like cat urine".<br />
Aventus is undoubtedly a nice masculine scent, it balances salty citrus and smokey accords perfectly, a beautiful fruity pineapple and citrus opening drying to a smokey masculine leathery dry down <br />
Truth be told, this is better than most niche fragrances, performance isn't even bad either.<br />
In my opinion this is the second best creed fragrance, above aventus cologne but slightly under silver mountain water, try it obviously first but this is a great cologne.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2272368"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2272368#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272097" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2272097" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Samurai23"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1536719"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1536719.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Samurai23" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2272097ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2272097" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1536719">Samurai23</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-05">09/05/24 01:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Recently bought my first Aventus. Lot F001397, so it's from the latest batches. I sampled it before that and the only concern at this point was longevity and sillage. The way I test a perfume is to spray it a couple of times on a piece of paper and leave it in a closed room or corridor at home and then go in and out every now and then. I don't sniff the piece of paper up close. The cloud is what matters. <br />
This way I test the perfume objectively, I know I'm not going nose blind, I ignore skin chemistry variations and experience the fragrance how 95% of people around me would experinece it.<br />
The result from my new bottle was that for the first 3 hours the room smelled beautifully of pineapple. The pineapple slowly fades during that time. After that, for the next 3-4 hours, the pineapple has slowly faded into the smoky-woody drydown. The drydown fills the room initially and at around the 6th hour is detectable within arm's reach. But it is detectable.<br />
Around the 8-9th hour, the scent was still there but barely.... somebody hugging you would notice it.<br />
But I like to think conservatively. Let' say it lasts for 6 hours. Overall, I'm pleased with this performance. <br />
Your satisfaction will depend on your expectations. For me, this is a special fragrance for special occasions or at least not an everyday fragrance. And for such a perfume you would spray it before going out and expecting to be where you need to be within half an hour to an hour. This leaves you plenty of time to project.<br />
If your expectation is that the perfume will last a long time because it is expensive... yes and no. Price doesn't directly correlate with longevity/sillage. Type and quality of ingredients, bottle and presentation are just some of the variables... you get the picture...</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2272097"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2272097#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2271635" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2198763">rickgrit</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-04">09/04/24 14:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Aventus, CDNIM (Club) and Montblanc Explorer tested side by side: Aventus most refined, Explorer very close behind in all respects.  Club a nauseous, lemon pledge opening that calms down in 30 - 45 minutes but still a very rough scent throughout.  Longevity and sillage about the same for the former two, Club's is well beyond that - albeit an inferior and annoying scent.  Montblanc Explorer the easy choice here - Aventus' price is obscene for the return; Club is strong and annoying irrespective of the price and compliments.  I don't want to smell it on me.  In fact, I don't want to smell it on you!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2271635"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2271635#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2271224" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1291437">Ferg1</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-04">09/04/24 07:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Out of all the reformulations that have been made on all famous fragrances, the downgrade on this one is simply unbeatable, congrats Erwin.<br />
<br />
This is nothing anymore, just citruses, that disappear in a heart beat.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2271224"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2271224#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2270175" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2270175" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Zongo"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1559457"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1559457.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Zongo" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2270175ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2270175" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1559457">Zongo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-03">09/03/24 09:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Listen up, you patchouli-soaked degenerates. We're about to dive headfirst into the twisted world of Creed's Aventus, a fragrance that's supposed to make you smell like Napoleon if he'd been dipped in a vat of fruit cocktail and rolled through a cedar forest.<br />
<br />
They tell me this is the Holy Grail of men's fragrances. Well, I've seen my fair share of holy relics, and let me tell you, this ain't it, chief. This is more like the Wholly Disappointing, a shadow of its former self, limping along on the fumes of its past glory.<br />
<br />
I sprayed this "F batch" on my wrist, expecting to be transported to the battlefields of Austerlitz. Instead, I found myself in a cut-rate farmer's market, drowning in a sea of overripe grapefruits. For 45 minutes, I reeked like a citrus truck that had overturned on a hot highway. And then? Nothing. Nada. Zilch. It vanished faster than a politician's campaign promises after election day.<br />
<br />
Where's the smoke? Where's the leather? Where's the goddamn birch that's supposed to make you smell like you've been rolling around in a forest fire? It's gone, baby. Gone like a snowball in Death Valley.<br />
<br />
They say if you want the real deal, you've got to huff some knock-off called Club de Nuit Intense Man. Can you believe it? The clone is more authentic than the original. It's like finding out your doppelganger is living a better version of your life.<br />
<br />
This, my friends, is the state of modern perfumery. We're chasing ghosts, trying to recapture the glory of scents past. Aventus isn't just a fragrance anymore, it's a cautionary tale. A reminder that even the mightiest can fall, reduced to a pale imitation of their former selves.<br />
<br />
So save your hard-earned greenbacks, unless you're in the market for the world's most expensive grapefruit air freshener. In this cruel circus of olfactory delights, sometimes the best move is to stick with the imposters. At least they're honest about their deception.<br />
<br />
And remember, in a world gone mad with reformulations and watered-down legends, the only winning move is to spray with extreme prejudice. Or better yet, roll around in a pile of pineapples and smoke a cedar log. You'll probably smell more like classic Aventus than this sorry excuse for a fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2270175"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2270175#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2266402" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2259279" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Thronumgoroth"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1410645"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1410645.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Thronumgoroth" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Issey-Miyake/L-Eau-d-Issey-Pour-Homme-Or-Encens-47155.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.47155.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="L’Eau d’Issey Pour Homme Or Encens"title="L’Eau d’Issey Pour Homme Or Encens"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2259279ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2259279" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1410645">Thronumgoroth</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-24">08/24/24 05:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is one of the most unfortunate fragrances in my collection for the following reasons:<br />
<br />
- By the time I got this scent, I had already amassed a sizeable collection and had grown into a seasoned nose.<br />
- There is no way the scent can live up to the hype the internet creates because truth of the matter is, this scent's reputation very usually preceeds it landing in the hands of collectors.<br />
<br />
When I initially got this fragrance, I was slightly disappointed and found it quite basic and uninteresting. With more wears, I grown a little fond of it and I find myself missing it after long stints of not wearing it. It is pleasant, versitile and I dare say, very classy. Suitable for practically every occasion - From casual summer days, to dressed up winter dinners and everything inbetween. For all of it's positives, there are very obvious and some very well known drawbacks like the performance - For the premium this scent demands, the performance is quite dissappointing. The sillage and projection are minimal, with this only extending a small scent bubble around you on initial spray and drawing closer to the skin as it dries down with people sometimes needing to breach your personal space for the scent to greet them. In terms of longetivity, I found it to very casually hit around 8 - 10 hours, so I have no complaints there. <br />
<br />
If the scent was not as expensive as it is, I would very easily recommend it, not only to  avid collectors, but also to people that are new to our collecting culture. Perhaps there was a time where this was the king of perfumes, but today, that is not the case. The more experienced with fragrance may even find this to be rather mediocre and uninteresting.<br />
<br />
Overall, here is my rating:<br />
Scent: 6.5 or 7/10<br />
Pricing: 3/10<br />
Versatility: 8/10<br />
Longevity: 7/10<br />
Projection: 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2259279"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2259279#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2257987" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2257987" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Wheresmybeer"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/893768"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Wheresmybeer" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2257987ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2257987" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/893768">Wheresmybeer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-22">08/22/24 23:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My favourite fragrance of all time.. People that are saying this is overhyped, &amp; not unique with bad performance are obviously smelling newer batches.. <br />
<br />
This got all its hype from older batches, &amp; when it was released &amp; it was unique, nothing smelt like it.. Now it’s been cloned a million times so the smell is no longer unique.. <br />
<br />
The proper Aventus before it got ruined with reformulation were the older 120ml &amp; 75ml bottles before they changed to 100ml &amp; 50ml bottles..I have a few of the older bottles &amp; it performs beastly.. I have tried the later reformulation &amp; it is now a shadow of what it once was.. So if you buy this, remember the hype was from before reformulation, and it’s hype for the pre- reformulation was well deserved.. <br />
<br />
It’s a shame like many great fragrances it has been ruined with reformulation… <br />
<br />
Old batches before reformulation 10/10<br />
New batches reformulated 5/10 ( and I’m being very generous with that 5)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2257987"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2257987#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2257883" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137868">EmilZakaryan924</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-22">08/22/24 19:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tried an old batch of this from 2016 when I visited a family member. Super iconic DNA that is well blended and a mass appealing masterpiece. I haven't tried the new formulations of this but most people say it doesn't last at all anymore. Starts off fruity, citrusy, leathery, smoky and fresh. Dry down is more focused on the leather and smokiness and less citruses and fruits. Super nice fragrance but it's not worth its price tag of 300-500 USD. <br />
<br />
Let's talk about the performance. With this batch I got around 8-9 hours on my skin with a medium projection leaning masculine. This is a somewhat versatile fragrance for the spring, summer and maybe the fall. It's a bit weaker in its current formulation ( accord to the internet ) so its weakest season is winter. You can technically wear this in the day and night, to work, dressed up, or dressed down. <br />
<br />
Lastly, is it a safe blind buy? If you have the money for it, go ahead. But with the numerous amount of dupes for this, kinda makes this overpriced. I have never tried any Aventus clone like Club de Nuit Intense Man but I am sure they are very similar to this. <br />
<br />
In conclusion: <br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Longevity ( older formulation ): 8/10<br />
Projection: ( older formulation ): 7/10<br />
<br />
Creed Aventus: 8.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2257883"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2257883#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2254118" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2251480" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="brha"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1840715"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1840715.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="brha" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Comme-des-Garcons/Comme-des-Garcons-Series-6-Synthetic-Soda-1238.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1238.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Comme des Garcons Series 6 Synthetic: Soda"title="Comme des Garcons Series 6 Synthetic: Soda"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2251480ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2251480" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1840715">brha</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-16">08/16/24 12:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Unfortunately, I fell victim to the hype with this one. Got a couple bottles and felt disappointed everytime. Expectations were high. Too high. I let the hype influence my expectations. I swore off Creed all together for all the common reasons for years. Then...my father in law offered me a few sprays of his nearly empty bottle (what a guy!). It got it's hooks in. I needed a bottle and I'm glad to have one again. The clones and dupes have never done it for me. <br />
It's a legend for a reason.<br />
I'm going to take the lazy approach and agree with the reviewer below for smell etc. However, I want to add there's a slight effervescence or sparkle to the real deal; add in the clean musk and vanilla tones and it's addictive. <br />
Aaron Terence Hughes has described  Creed as light, airy, and great sillage. I think that's part of the magic here but also part of the curse. Light, airy, and effervescent usually also mean performance will suffer. Every clone I've tried has been more dense with better performance but lack the structure and sparkle. <br />
Batches...its truly a thing...to a degree. By that I mean you won't find crazy differences with modern batches. However, join an Aventus FB group etc and try to get a decant of say a 2015 (or older) vs modern. You will understand then. I enjoy the older batches I've tried but the modern batches are brighter and imo more mass appealing. The vintage batches will vary but are more bottom heavy...smoke, anise, and woods. 10/10 from a former Creed hater.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2251480"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2251480#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2250351" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2250351" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="mixthemix"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2222540"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="mixthemix" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2250351ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2250351" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2222540">mixthemix</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-15">08/15/24 11:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The Scent that Conquers All (Except My Wallet)<br />
<br />
If you ever find yourself wandering through a fragrance store, lost in a haze of floral notes and Old Spice, let me introduce you to Creed’s Aventus — also known as “The Scent of Success” and “Why Is My Bank Account Crying?” This gem is essentially a fragrance for those who whispered sweet nothings to their bank managers and now fancy themselves successful entrepreneurs… or just someone who can finally afford more than ramen noodles for dinner.<br />
<br />
**The Smell:** Imagine if a dapper, suave man-bear—think bear in a tuxedo—decided to take a luxurious bath in a blend of pineapple, birch, and a touch of mystery. That’s Aventus for you. It opens with a boldness that screams, “I mean business” (preferably business class), yet it also softens into an irresistible charm that would make even your grandma consider taking you out for ice cream.<br />
<br />
**Longevity:** The scent lingers like your favorite uncle at a party who just won’t leave — in the best way possible. You’ll walk past the grocery store and notice shoppers turning their heads like they’ve just caught a glimpse of a celebrity. “Is that… did he just walk by?” Yes, my friend, that’s the power of Aventus. You’ll have to start carrying around a tiny scent-locking vault because this fragrance will have people following you.<br />
<br />
**Compliments:** Expect compliments faster than a cat video goes viral. Stranger: “You smell amazing! What is that?” You: *proudly* “Oh, just a little something I picked up… it’s called Aventus.” Suddenly, you’re standing in a circle of admirers, sharing anecdotes while subtly letting them know that yes, you, too, can now afford groceries from the organic section.<br />
<br />
**Price Tag:** Now, let’s address the elephant in the room — the price. Aventus costs about as much as a rent payment in a hipster neighborhood. You’ll find yourself contemplating, “Should I buy it or pay my car insurance this month?” Chances are, you’ll choose Aventus and yell “YOLO!” as your car sits forlornly in the driveway, hoping for a miracle.<br />
<br />
**Overall Rating: 9/10 — (1 point deducted for financial crisis)**<br />
<br />
In conclusion, if you’re looking to smell like a thousand-dollar bill in a crisp suit, look no further than Creed’s Aventus. Just remember — while it may attract admirers, it will also attract the attention of your credit card company in ways you never anticipated. But hey, at least you’ll smell like a conqueror! Happy spritzing!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2250351"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2250351#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2249220" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2221374">Esaf Mahmuti</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-14">08/14/24 01:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Probably the most influental men's perfume in this millenium, it's hard to describe the scent but definitely it's ultimate mass-pleasant.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2248635"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2248635#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2247417" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1698745">romanGM</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-12">08/12/24 23:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This DNA is present nearly everywhere, but most clones that people mention like CDNI and Supremacy Silver are, yes, close, but place too much emphasis on the smokiness and dense side of Aventus in my personal preference. <br />
I have a tiny bit left in my bottle, its a lovely fresh juicy pineapple scent with a hint of smoke for me, so I'll probably only visit it when I'm really in the mood.<br />
<br />
Would I buy a new bottle? Probably not, depends how much I miss it. <br />
Is there a reason the DNA is so popular in the fragrance world? Yes.<br />
Do clones capture the essence of Aventus? Kind of?<br />
But is getting the extra 15% worth £200 of your money? Depends how much you're willing to spend. <br />
<br />
Cool asf bottle tho. But I think Creed stands true to it's motto or whatever "From Father to Son", bought as a gift to mark a milestone and make the bottle last, not OMG I love this fragrance I'm going to always use it and buy it 5x over. <br />
<br />
Aventus summed up in one word: Iconic.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2247417"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2247417#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2247395" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2247395" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="OU812M8"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2215970"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="OU812M8" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2247395ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2247395" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2215970">OU812M8</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-12">08/12/24 22:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Review based on my Sep 2021 bottle (Batch Code: L4221S01)<br />
<br />
Creed Aventus has long been hailed as a masterpiece in the fragrance world, and for good reason. The scent itself is undeniably captivating, a perfect blend of fruity, smoky, and woody notes that exudes confidence and sophistication. This was my go-to spring/summer fragrance for special occasions.<br />
<br />
However, I’ve had my 2021 bottle for a while now, and I have to say, I’m disappointed, it hasn’t seemed to get stronger with maceration at all, contrary to what others have said. While the scent profile remains solid (minus the birch), the performance and sillage have noticeably declined in comparison to older batches. What once lasted for hours and projected beautifully now seems to fade far too quickly, leaving me questioning whether it’s truly worth the hefty price tag.<br />
<br />
Given the wealth of above-average clones like Mont Blanc Explorer at a fraction of the cost, I think this will be my last bottle of Aventus. It’s unfortunate because the fragrance itself is still a classic, but if it can’t perform like it used to, why pay the premium?<br />
<br />
For those new to Aventus, it’s worth experiencing at least once, but buy a sample, cause if you’re looking for something that offers good longevity and projection, you might want to explore other options such as Explorer or if you wanna go niche try Mancera's Cedrat Boise (not a clone but similar profile to Aventus). <br />
<br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Longevity: 3/10<br />
Projection: 3/10<br />
Price: 2/10<br />
Overall: 4/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2247395"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2247395#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2246953" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Overrated, overpriced and weak performance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2235209"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2235209#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2234466" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It’s iconic, but at this point absurdly priced and a bit inconsistent in performance. I find a lot of clones can match the fruity citrus pineapple opening but lack the same smoothness and mossy base. The base is a modern chypre that ties it to classic masculine scents many of us (who aren’t babies) smelled growing up but added a new dimension that changed the fragrance landscape after its release. This scent (or any) will not save you from a questionable hygiene or if you're poorly dressed. It works in the form of a full package. <br />

It’s okay ✅ to me if you don’t notice, therefore I hope there is no sillage. When I was less sillage was all-important. A sign that some important elements of toilet had been accomplished.
