padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1434113">DeFraghead</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-10">07/10/24 02:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>While Creed Aventus is often praised for its unique pineapple note and longevity, I found it to be overly hyped and underwhelming. The opening blast of fruitiness was pleasant, but it quickly faded into a generic, overly synthetic dry down on my skin. Considering its high price point, I expected more complexity and richness in its composition. Overall, I was disappointed with the performance and expected more depth from a fragrance with such a strong reputation.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2213828"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2213828#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2213810" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1856996">slow_burn</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-04">07/04/24 11:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>You know by now that Aventus is one of the most extraordinarily beautiful fragrances ever created. You're only reading reviews because you're trying to justify shelling out $275.00-$400.00 for a bottle of something that people are calling a skin scent that disappears after one hour because it's allegedly been ruined through multiple reformulations over the years.<br />
<br />
I got my bottle in November 2023. Of course it smelled amazing as soon as I opened it, but after about 4 months of maturation, performance improved drastically to about 3 hours while projecting to around 6 feet. Now with nearly 8 months of maturation people smell it on me about 5 hours later. It's also by far my biggest compliment getter. Both men and women at work, hotels, restaurants and even the grocery store have told me "you smell really good."<br />
<br />
If you're on the fence, buy at least a 2 ml decant.  Try it and then put it away and try it again a few months later when you're going to go out and see how you feel about it then. Many of the people leaving bad reviews have never owned at least a decent sized sample. Trashing a fragrance after spraying it from a friend's bottle, a perfume counter or a test strip is meaningless. You should smell it on your skin a few times, months apart and then decide.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2208161"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2208161#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2207252" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2200571" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="BDK"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1778793"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1778793.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="BDK" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Maison-Francis-Kurkdjian/Gentle-Fluidity-Silver-53400.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.53400.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gentle Fluidity Silver"title="Gentle Fluidity Silver"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2200571ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2200571" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1778793">BDK</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-26">06/26/24 20:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Received a 15ml decant from a very trusted discounter I have used many times. I have tried CDNIM and L’aventure and they never quite did it for me, but I was a fan of explorer the couple times I tested it. I got a decant of the real deal to see what this DNA is all about. Have to say I’m quite disappointed. <br />
       After the 2 minutes of lemon-cleaner-death you get on the opening of CDNIM, it’s 95% Aventus. I can’t speak on older batches, but the ‘24/‘23 version is just barely different. Obviously a smoother opening, and ever so slightly smoother overall during the heart and dry down (I basically have to talk myself into this notion to notice anything different whatsoever), on skin after 20-30 minutes I simply cannot tell a difference. Don’t get me wrong, I think this DNA is incredibly clever and creed came up with an iconic masterpiece. But if a 30 dollar clone can get THIS close, there is an issue with pricing. <br />
<br />
     I’m quite critical on the differences between clones and the real thing and usually pickup at least a few obvious differences, but in this situation the main clones (CDNIM and l’aventure) are basically indistinguishable from current aventus batches after the 2 minute initial opening. charging 500 retail and 250+ at discounters is pure comedy. From what I gather this fragrance has diminished in quality all while increasing the prices 50+ percent over the past several years. I actually prefer explorer for this profile overall as I think it tends to fit a younger man like myself a bit better. I bought an aventus clone for my father who is in that 45-55 range and he loves it, and frankly I think it suits that age range best, but that’s just opinion. Very versatile, masculine, bold, fresh. FWIW I actually think the performance of Aventus is not nearly as bad as what people say. Seems to jump off my skin and I can pick it up in the air 2-3 hours after application and 6-7 on skin. Pretty run if the mill EDP performance I’d say. <br />
        Overall, not worth the price. Please try both first and decide for yourself but frankly I would NEVER reccomend Aventus over CDNIM or L’aventure, even if the creed was at 100-150, that extra 2-5% of smoothness is just simply not worth it. The DNA is identical.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2200571"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2200571#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2199809" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2197004" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SniffDogg"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2016536"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2016536.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SniffDogg" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Armaf/Legesi-Homme-52265.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.52265.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Legesi Homme"title="Legesi Homme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2197004ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2197004" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2016536">SniffDogg</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-23">06/23/24 05:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Finally got my paws on a decant sample sprayer of Aventus, after trying most of the clones out there. Most of the clones are extremely similar, maybe a slightly different wood smell in the background or a little bit sweeter like L'Aventure. <br />
<br />
But the 2 clones that are indistinguishable from the real Creed Aventus are......Armaf Club De Nuit Intense Man (CDNIM) and surprisingly Cremo Bergamot and Musk. They both smell exactly like Aventus, I would not be able to tell they were not real Aventus in a blind test. The only difference between the 2 clones is strength/longevity. <br />
<br />
CDNIM is very strong, I would treat it like the parfum version or EDP, while Bergamot and Musk has good sillage but more like a regular EDT. I bought a full bottle of B&amp;M, and it's good for mainly around the house. If I keep wearing this cologne I'll probably get a bottle of CDNIM too at some point and go light on the sprays. <br />
<br />
Overall I think that Aventus is like 95% bergamot, all the other little notes are very fleeting or not noticeable. Sometimes I smell smoky wood for 2 seconds in the opening and it's gone. So what does bergamot smell like? I would describe it as 1/3 lemon and 2/3 lime. Lots of colognes have bergamot in them, but I guess maybe Aventus was the first to feature it so heavily?<br />
<br />
In the end I guess I'm happy that Aventus does not smell different or better than the clones, I don't want to try and afford $500 bottles of cologne! I would have to get a job as a K9 cop or something. I'm currently rotating Bergamot and Musk, Versace Pour Homme, and Nautica Voyage. For the late fall and winter I'm going to pick up a bottle of Burberry London for men.<br />
<br />
So in conclusion is it worth it to buy Creed Aventus? No, not unless you're very wealthy and spending hundreds on a single cologne is no problem for you. Those 2 clones I mentioned are exact matches and I think they're high quality.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2197004"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2197004#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2195780" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Smell wise it's one of best things I ever smelled, but for the price 300€+ I would give max 6.5/10 overall.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2193379"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2193379#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2192501" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2192501" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Makes2MuchScents"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1787230"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1787230.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Makes2MuchScents" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2192501ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2192501" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1787230">Makes2MuchScents</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-18">06/18/24 18:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Decent frag. <br />
<br />
You can't really go wrong with it. But I would say that Creed has more frags for ppl to consume that are just as great or even better than this. Sounds like blasphemy to everyone that wants to wear a frag to be like everyone else. But it is true. For instance, I believe that Creed Erolfa is greater than this I would also so that Virgin Island Water is better. In fact, I have received more compliments on those two than I have ever with Aventus. <br />
<br />
Also, I have received more compliments on Club De Nuit than Aventus (hot take). But unlike most, I wear the fragrances I like to wear for me--compliments are just a part of the fragrance journey that I could care less about. <br />
<br />
Lastly the 10-year anniversary is simply for collectors (for those who are curious or new to the frag game and wanted to know) and Absolu is actually nicer than the OG Aventus to me, but I would still not pay retail for it only because it's like Creed is just trying to stretch the clout of what Aventus has garnered. I do not see a reason to purchase older bottles of Aventus either for the wild prices frag heads are selling them for. Not hating at all, your paper, but a 500+ after market price tag for an OG bottle simply becasue it has more Birch or Pineapple is just wild. Especially since the frag is still being produced and yeah it may be little differences here and there but never enough to spend a crazy amount for what I mentioned. <br />
<br />
Cheers matey!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2192501"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2192501#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2191384" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1043744">FreshLiving</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-17">06/17/24 19:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I’m a creed fanboy through and through. They make the best scents on the market by a LONG shot. Always classy, refined, uplifting, clean, with personality. <br />
<br />
I’ve been reading a lot over the years how Aventus has been watered down and doesn’t perform. So I was at the boutique this weekend buying a bottle of Neroli Savaige in Holt Renfrew and decided to spritz my arm with Green Irish Tweed and Aventus while she was readying my purchase. <br />
<br />
I do not lie and I can afford these fragrances, but the performance on this, was truly terrible. It barely projected and was a faint skin scent truly in 1.5 hours. The GIT was performing quietly for 3 hours and then receded quite quickly too. And then I had neroli on my other arm and it was still going well in to the night (it’s not a projector but the longevity in it goes for like 10-12 hours) and when I went for a workout the next morning it turned back on and projected. So that one probably does quite well in heat.<br />
<br />
Back to the point; they have changed this magical juice. And it is no longer worth it. I don’t get why Creed is watering their products down, but they are altering them too much. <br />
<br />
Aventus and GIT, based on their ingredients should be performing quite well and noticeable to the wearer without searching for it, for at least 8 hours. It’s deeply unfortunate for creed enthusiasts like myself that both of these last for only a couple hours. <br />
<br />
I have a 2016 bottle of this that I will use sparingly because I doubt the old Aventus that made this brand what it is today, is not coming back… Unless you can become a celebrity and have a special batch made just for you that is.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2179326"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2179326#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2178907" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2178907" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="danilodeathayde"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1620729"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1620729.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="danilodeathayde" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2178907ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2178907" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1620729">danilodeathayde</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-05">06/05/24 10:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>(Evaluation made with a 1ml decant)<br />
<br />
Not worth the investment for a Brazilian by any stretch. If it wasn't an issue with my decant ordered from King of Decants, the performance is almost as poor as a Blue Seduction or Montblanc Legend.<br />
<br />
The scent itself is very pleasant if you smell it within the first 20 minutes after spraying, but then it fades quickly. The pineapple disappears, leaving a smoky, musky pleasantness, but it’s quite generic for the contemporary olfactory ethos. Even this base doesn't stay perceptible for more than an hour.<br />
<br />
All the "wow" factor of the perfume, in my perception, seems to be in its opening, but it's too ephemeral. I would still venture to say that the sharper acidity of Club de Nuit Intense remains more interesting in its development, although it is evidently more artificial than the note of Creed.<br />
<br />
Club de Nuit exudes and remains more noticeable for longer, maintaining the same profile as Creed. However, it would be worth comparing the two side by side with Montblanc Explorer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2178907"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2178907#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2178206" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2178206" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Cuir et Santal"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2156106"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2156106.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Cuir et Santal" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Royal-Oud-12317.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.12317.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Royal Oud"title="Royal Oud"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2178206ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2178206" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2156106">Cuir et Santal</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-04">06/04/24 17:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>**Be warned: a total 'box-dropper'**<br />
<br />
I'm not going to wax lyrical about the particular notes, as I think that's well covered both in reviews and by the pyramid above, so I'll just get into it:<br />
<br />
This scent is incredible. It smells amazing, and any man who has ever smelled it will probably say the same. Herein lies the problem.<br />
<br />
I have been complimented on this scent every time I've worn it, multiple times, every time. And every compliment was from a man. Women just don't like it as much. Many women I've spoken to loathe it, and say it smells weirdly feminine on men.<br />
<br />
I can only recommend this one if you're having a round a golf with the lads from work, and you want them all to think you're cool, sophisticated, and dominant. And they probably will. If you're a homosexual male, then do wear this on dates. I've done so a few times with men I've been on dates with, and they love it. Alternatively, get it if you want to wear it for yourself and smell it all day, regardless of how it makes you come across. It does smell magnificent.<br />
<br />
Otherwise, avoid it like the plague. You don't smell as sleek and sexy as you think. Not to women, at least.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2178206"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2178206#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2176926" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; So I will summarize my own comment by saying that there's absolutely nothing wrong with enjoying all the "smell-alikes" out there. Whether it be for the price difference, or maybe you genuinely prefer whatever clone you're rocking to the original. I certainly own and love some clones myself.<br />
But make no mistake..<br />
<br />
This -IS- the Original.<br />
And so,  there's ALSO absolutely nothing wrong with wanting to wear the top quality of the original.<br />
And Top quality it is.<br />
The obvious quality of that birchwood, smoke, and pineapple is what did me in!  👌</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2176158"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2176158#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2176096" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It’s amazing, but it’s not worth $300+.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2170586"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2170586#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2168858" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2168858" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="banksia"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1568248"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1568248.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="banksia" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Royal-Princess-Oud-31563.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.31563.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Royal Princess Oud"title="Royal Princess Oud"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2168858ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2168858" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1568248">banksia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-26">05/26/24 20:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Take all the typical notes of male leaning fragrances - aromatic, citrus, sweet fruit, leather, tobacco, wood - and put them into one fragrance that shifts between them over time, and you have Aventus. The initial spray of light aromatic and citrus notes lasted about 1-2 hours, becoming sweeter and revealing that pineapple scent. The dry down was substantially more leathery and smoky than I expected, almost reminding me of LV Ombre Leather. I've had a couple compliments on this one, with people mostly complimenting the muskier side of the fragrance. At this price tag, I'm really looking for better performance, and I think the scent plays it too safe with nothing that really stands out and makes it memorable. I feel like Aventus will always be the Sauvage of the niche fragrance world for that reason.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2168858"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2168858#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2168069" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2168069" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Mydaus"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1765171"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Mydaus" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2168069ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2168069" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1765171">Mydaus</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-26">05/26/24 00:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let me preface this by stating that I have previously bought a 10ml sample of the Armaf clone and after using that up I was not very impressed with it. Although performance was strong, there was something in the proportions of the different notes that wasn’t quite correct for me and I really didn’t like it. <br />
I decided that I wanted to try the real thing to see if it was actually any different so I ordered a genuine Aventus 10ml sample to try. <br />
This is a whole different animal altogether.<br />
I can see the similarities but it’s like saying a Ford is like a Ferrari in that it has four wheels and doors and a seat and steering wheel.<br />
The first thing I noticed with Aventus is the quality of the opening. The pineapple fruit is much more pronounced here, as are the other fruity notes. The whole thing just smells more smooth and luxurious. The ingredients are obviously of a much higher quality than in the clones.<br />
A scent like this is easy to copy the basics, but it’s in the details that make it what it is. The notes are correctly in proportion to each other and it makes for a much better blend.<br />
Creed have nailed it with this fragrance, I didn’t expect to like it as much as I do. That said, it isn’t appropriate for all situations and to me this is an evening/going out type of fragrance. <br />
Performance is solid 5hrs. <br />
It would be interesting to try different “batches” and discover how different they actually are.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2168069"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2168069#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2167892" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;     <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent756587" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc756587" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Raidthesaladbar"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/659619"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.659619.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Raidthesaladbar" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma756587ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd756587" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/659619">Raidthesaladbar</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2016-10-29">10/29/16 08:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ah, Aventus… Not even Creed's laughably inflated prices could stop you from becoming a bestseller, even beyond the usual demographic of niche aficionados. For years, Creed fans used to look down on the peasants wearing Cool Water (considered a dumbed-down version of their beloved Green Irish Tweed). Now they've been somewhat undercut, as Johnny Cargopants and his fratbro entourage have forsaken their Davidoff and started touring the clubs with a cloud of Aventus trailing behind them. <br />
<br />
Since there's not much I could add to describe the fragrance itself, I feel I should instead answer some of the more pressing questions I've come across on the BN Aventus subforums.<br />
<br />
1. Yes, Aventus is a chick magnet. You'll be the center of attention at any bar or club. Nevermind the two dozen other dudes around you who are also doused in pineapple. They're probably wearing that self-made knockoff recipe of Club de Nuit Intense and apple soda you saw on Youtube (which you totally didn't try). You'll be way cooler, wearing the real thing and sipping on the Snapple juicebox you brought from home.<br />
<br />
2. There's plenty of websites that sell Aventus at a discount (look for those which have authentic Ray-Bans at 90% off). But the cheapest way to get it is the so-called "unlimited pre-evening trial". How it works: Hit your favourite Sephora 5 minutes before closing time, and tell them you wanna “try” Aventus. If you’re afraid the saleslady is onto you (because she sees you coming in every Friday evening before you hit the clubs), try buttoning your shirt and tucking in your chest hair. <br />
<br />
3. On the subject of dosage: If you still blow below the legal limit after dousing your body in pineapple-scented alcohol, you haven’t sprayed enough. Go back in and tell the saleslady you accidentally sprayed the wrong tester. Have your friend Johnny stand next to you, so she’ll think the miasma of tropical fruit is emanating from his slightly damp cargo pants.   <br />
 <br />
4. Yes, Aventus is indeed the most original fragrance to come along in years. Every other fruity, smoky or woody fragrance thereafter has obviously been inspired by it, so make sure to mention that in your reviews of those fragrances. It even applies to older scents of those types, because Aventus has clearly outclassed them. For extra points, bring that up when discussing a classic that’s known to have its own rabidly devoted fanbase (try Guerlain’s Mitsouko).<br />
<br />
5. A true Aventus man knows his batch codes, and can recommend the right batch for any occasion. Hot date at your favourite club? Try one of the smokier batches from way back (2011). Fun day at the mall with your bros, shopping for new cargo pants? One of the fruitier batches will put you in the right mood. When in doubt, consult the experts who stash vintage bottles and regularly compare them to current batches. Rumour has it that the juice people spit into buckets at Aventus tastings is used as the base for Dior’s Sauvage. <br />
    <br />
Aventus is love. Aventus is life. Long live Aventus.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="756587"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=756587#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent386806" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc386806" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="browne54"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/442472"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="browne54" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Guerlain/Habit-Rouge-Eau-de-Toilette-16.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.16.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Habit Rouge Eau de Toilette"title="Habit Rouge Eau de Toilette"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma386806ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd386806" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/442472">browne54</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2013-07-15">07/15/13 18:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>HOLY. SHIT. and I stress the Holy. This  is the first fragrance where I have literally been mesmerized. I had smelled GIT by Creed. Wasnt impressed for the price. Millesime Imperial, which I like a lot, but not for the price. After those two I just wrote off the Creed House as overpriced and not worth the products produced. However, I was strolling through Neiman Marcus and gave this one a try in attempts to crush the what I was certain to be hype. I was so taken aback I shouted "My God" out loud in the store. I have NEVER smelled anything quite like this. Never. So incredibly unique. Inspired by Napoleon? I believe it. It smells like power. I understand that is an obnoxious statement but congruent with my reaction and the perfume's inspiration.<br />
<br />
Up top: pineapple. and fresh cut, real, not synthetic pineapple. I detect a hint of black currant.<br />
<br />
Middle: starts to get smokey. I detect birch all the way. Birch and patchouli with a hint of rose. God it is so wonderful.<br />
<br />
Base: an oakmoss/leather base. It says leather is not a note but I think the oakmoss/musk/fading fruits make some type of leather accord. Divine. Literally.<br />
<br />
Longevity: I got 9 hours on my skin and it was projecting for 5-6.<br />
<br />
I walked out of Neiman Marcus with Aventus on my hand, to check it with my chemistry, to meet my gf in the hair salon. I walked into a wall of compliments. Every woman in the salon was in awe. Walk out of the salon, a male stranger passes, walks back to me and taps me on the shoulder to ask what cologne I was wearing. That has never happened in my life. I intend to purchase the 4.0oz after my next pay period as well as the shave balm. Before smelling Aventus I would have thought I was outside of my mind to purchase a $300 fragrance. But I believe it is because I know my search for my perfect/signature scent is over. I will always have a few staples in the collection; Fahrenheit, Encre Noire, Dior Homme Intense for romantic evenings. But I can never see myself liking anything more, or feeling anything suits who I am better than Aventus. And I must say, it is a beautiful thing. This is the best fragrance I have EVER smelled. Breathtakingly beautiful and seductively powerful.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="386806"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=386806#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1478521" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1478521" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TuxedoMan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1426745"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1426745.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TuxedoMan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Original-Cologne-Pure-White-Cologne-13391.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.13391.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Original Cologne (Pure White Cologne)"title="Original Cologne (Pure White Cologne)"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1478521ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1478521" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1426745">TuxedoMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-01-07">01/07/22 16:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There is a lot of talk about Creed Aventus and the infamous batch variations and reformulations (?).<br />
First of all, let me say that I am wearing Aventus since 2015 and have owned and used 4 different bottles over the past 5 years. I just finished my older bottle this week, a vintage 2013 batch (13W01), I have used a 2015 one (don't know because I didn't care for the batches back then), a 16E01 (2016), a 50ml bottle of 17R01 (my favourite) and have a 20E01N sitting as a backup for a year now.<br />
I love them all! Yes they do smell SLIGHTLY different. You can DEFINITELY notice it, altough in the air they basically smell the same, like Aventus of course! But, to me, that's one of the most interesting and magical things of Aventus. It has a life of it's own. You will find 3 different "sides" of Aventus: you have the SMOKY side; the BALANCED batches; and the FRUITY side.<br />
A SMOKY batch will have stronger notes of birch and musk, the woody an leather accords are more prounced in those batches and it will feel heavier, more dense, smokier .. that's what a smoky Aventus is. With that density usually comes a little more longevity. That more pronounced leather accord from those batches is where people get the similarities with Mancera's Cedrat Boise from (not all Aventus have that - it is subtle though ..).<br />
The BALANCED batches are great to my nose. Exactly what the name suggests, a more balanced composition where none it's different sides shout louder. From my experience the batches that are well balanced have the strongest projection and a really beautiful scent trail and sillage. The vanilla in the drydown is to die for. Really beautiful.<br />
A FRUITIER batch is usually not as base notes dense as the others and have a brighter, fresher and frutier opening. It was only when I got one of these batches that I could clearly smell the apple and the bergamot. For the people who love freshies this is the perfect type of Aventus batch for you. The opening is so uplifting! I feel that the fruitier batches project really well for the first hours but then sit closer to the skin. Even with those I always get at least 8h longevity with Aventus (YES, even the newer 2020 batch).<br />
With all being said, please bear in mind that the same batch can also smell and performe differently with diffent Seasons of the year, temperatures, humidity, and of course in different skins.<br />
This is how Aventus as ALWAYS been through the years. It is a masterpiece fragrance. All those batch variations are completely normal and to be expected with the natural raw materials that the house of Creed is known for using. It can be off putting, of course, sometimes you don't know what you get. But fortunately, you can easily buy samples to try and test them first. And as I said, IT'S ALL AVENTUS. Those are small nuances, noticeable (sure) but minor, an untrained nose won't pick it up most of the times.<br />
What I would like to clarify here is the following: Aventus is as good now as with the older bottles. Please don't get caught into this batch variation rabbit hole. The performance is still there, the smell is the same (with the same batch variations), the quality of the ingredients is the same, the pacaking changes but only minor things, sprayer is great, it's all Aventus as we know it. What DID change is the price that is sky rocketing nowadays and that is what is pissing people off. If it's worth it, is up to you! If you look careful online you can find stores that sell the 50ml for arround 150-60 euros and the 100ml for 200 euros (that is acceptable for me). It's Aventus, it's pricey. We know that.<br />
Concluding, I finished my 2013 bottle this week and had a new 2020 bottle that I used for a week everyday and then let rest in the box for a whole year! AFTER that MACERATION time, I sprayed the 2013 batch on one hand and the 2020 on the other. The 2013 leans to the smokier side, and the 2020 batch is frutier. Both smell great like Aventus! 2020 lasted 12h on my skin and the 2013 lasted an extra hour and a half (total of 13,5 hours). The 2020 one projected more strongly for the first 3 to 4 hours mark and then became closer to the skin. The 2013 one sat closer to the skin during the wearing. I was very pleased with that. After that I gave them a full day wear and realized I like the new 2020 batch more then my prized vintage bottle. With all the batches from the bottles I have owned (and also bought a LOT of samples/decants along the years to try) my Aventus experience was always very similar: 8,5 to 14h of longevity (usually 12h); strong projection for the first 3 hours and always THAT AVENTUS DNA through years of wearing it. Please keep in mind that Creed fragrances are often linked with cases olfactory fatigue, specially Aventus. I fell that happening. It's not an easy fragrance to test, so if you are testing it don't keep trying to smell it all of the time and ask for other people to smell it. YOU WILL BE SURPRISED. Also notice that YOU CAN'T really compare a vintage older bottle to a brand new fresh one. It didn't have the time to age. And even if you leave it still macerating, you still can't compare bottle because of different maceration time. To make things worse with older bottles they can start going bad (specially the top notes). For sure they WILL go bad, it's just a matter of time. If you're looking for a good LAUGH look in forums for old threads about Creed batch variations. The batches people PRAISE NOW were also being THRASHED BACK THEN. Really, go look for it. It's a mind trap. The previous one is always better .. the vintage one, the unobtainable one is always be the holy grail .. "my neighbour's wife is better than mine" .. Come on, we are better than that.<br />
IN SUMMARY<br />
AVENTUS IS STILL AVENTUS! The quality, smell and performance are still there. Maceration time is a real thing and will bring the performance up. Test if for yourself if you can. The only problem with the actual Aventus is the price (it's going up!) but you can still find it new in stores for 200 euros for a 100ml bottle. That's an acceptable deal IMO. PLEASE save your self some time and money and don't go chasing for "magical" vintage or older bottles, clones or whatever. You want Aventus? It's NOT discontinued. It's up for sale. Just grab one. It's the same Aventus we love. Fragrances are to be worn, experienced, felt. If you love and want Aventus, just get it. I'ts a beautiful fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="1478521"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=1478521#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1198909" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1152847">Omniprime</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-07-12">07/12/20 13:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Aventus is a fragrance I always hated for years before even smelling it simply because of how much ridiculous hype it gets. Little did I know...it was fully worth the hype it got.<br />
<br />
When I finally decided to test it out, I was approaching it with a “I know I’ll hate this” mentality. However, I have caught myself sniffing my arm, clothes, and sprayer more times than I’d ever like to admit.<br />
<br />
And eventually, I just couldn’t resist, and pulled the trigger. And I was not disappointed one bit. From something I tried so hard to despise, to something I proudly call “my favorite fragrance of all time”.<br />
<br />
It is cloned to death, but no matter how good a clone is, nothing smells like Creed Aventus. <br />
<br />
While yes there is the batch-syndrome that Creed is well known for, I have tried over 5 different batches. Some where fruitier, some where smokier, but it does not matter. They are all very much the one and only Aventus.<br />
<br />
My main bottle is the infamous 2019 batch which enthusiast like to bash on, yet it still smells exceptional, and I actually prefer this newer batch over some of the older ones because it’s more balanced. But again, all Aventus are Aventus.<br />
<br />
People in the fragrance community say that the scent profile is too popular, however, I think there’s a misunderstanding here; the scent profile is too popular IN the fragrance community, but outside of it, barley anyone knows what Aventus is or what it smells like. And everyone I asked to try it out had their minds blown.<br />
<br />
 The one word that sums up everything about Aventus is: King.<br />
<br />
11/10, Legendary.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="1198909"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=1198909#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2127329" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2089916">Cabooter</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-17">04/17/24 07:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The craziest thing literally just happened. I have the habit of blind picking samples from my sample orders. This evening I put on a full 2 ml sample, about 20 sprays (I’m not a sissy sprayer) before going on a date. Immediately I am mesmerized by the fruity smoky cloud that hits me, it’s pure luxury.<br />
<br />
My date comes to pick me up at about 5 o’clock, she has pretty average smell compared to me. Whatever, I’m used to it. She was probably wearing some cheap designer stuff. When we start walking towards the car, I notice something peculiar. My date is leaving a snail-like gooey trail. Weird, I think, but get distracted by our conversation. In hindsight it was a precursor for what was about to come.<br />
<br />
When we enter the restaurant we get greeted by the waiter, whose eyes spread wide open the moment he enters my vicinity. “Good evening sir” he says “You have an amazing aura, you smell somewhat like a billionaire CEO”. Flattered by his comment I follow him towards our table, where a new waiter comes to take our order. “I sense an ‘old money’ atmosphere at this table, would you like to try our most expensive wine, for free?” Slightly surprised I comply. When he leaves I hear an overwhelming, slowly increasing wave of whispers coming from the entire restaurant. I can pick out phrases like “amazing projection”, “sigma male energy“, “incredibly sexy”, “absolutely not an NPC” and “a real panty-dropper”. I can barely focus on my date.<br />
<br />
Finally our food arrives. After I take my first bite, the whole restaurant starts clapping. I decide to take off my jacket because all this attention is making me feel overheated. This releases a beastmode tsunami of olfactory genius. A guy offers me his wife. One of the waitresses runs towards me from across the restaurant like a World War Z zombie, takes of her panties and shoves them in my mouth. My date jumps on the table, and screams “POWER!”. She starts beating her chest like a gorilla while squirting uncontrollably, flushing me out of the restaurant.<br />
<br />
I try to run home but a horde of at least 50 women is floating behind me sniffing my scent trail like loony tunes characters. They start picking at my skin like vultures. A guy in an all white suit and long blonde hair appears out of nowhere, takes my hand and transports me back to my house. He shows me the sample; “Bless yourself with this holy water”, he says. I look at the label, it reads “Creed Aventus”.<br />
<br />
Needless to say I immediately sold my least favorite colour Bugatti to buy 500 gallons of this absolute NICHE quality compliment MONSTER.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="2127329"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=2127329#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="9828" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

              10/10 for its popularity</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="145317"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=145317#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent574830" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I'm not saying everyone who enjoys Aventus is this way, but I believe most of the hype surrounding Aventus is the cost of the fragrance. Spending hundreds of dollars is supposedly "brag" worthy, I guess. It's a shame that people believe cost = quality. That's not always the case ESPECIALLY when it comes to fragrances and perfumery.<br />
<br />
Aventus is an ashy, bitter, musk cloud with heavy cat-piss/cat-urine accords (thanks to black currant + pineapple combo!).<br />
<br />
I remember inquiring about fruity fragrances way back in 2013 and multiple people had the audacity to recommend Aventus. Aventus is not fruity by any stretch. There is an occasional wisp of a super sweet pineapple note but it mostly contributes to the cat-urine accord that dominates Aventus along with the bitter ash accord.<br />
<br />
Calling Aventus a "fruity fragrance" because of one submissive note is like calling Acqua di Gio an "amber/balsamic fragrance" because it has amber in the basenotes.<br />
<br />
Try before you buy! If you genuinely like it (cost and popularity aside), congratulations!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="574830"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=574830#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent903656" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; What could possibly go wrong?<br />
<br />
Bleurgh, that's what. As soon as I sniffed this I realised it was the smell of every aggressive, overbearing, roid-raging, meat-headed, gym bunny type of guy I have ever backed away from (nervously) over the past decade. "Assertive" isn't in it - this is just the pure reek of the kind of man who truly believes "Ultimate Power" is a life goal! Him and his group of baying buddies all out on the town to paaaartaaaay, with their overgelled hair and their far-too-open shirts. <br />
<br />
My reaction is just violent antipathy. It was like one of Pavlov's dog experiments: I've been so conditioned over the years to just walk away from even a whiff this scent, because it's the smell of a hairy situation produced by testosterone overload on the drink-and-puke-sodden streets on any Friday night near you. <br />
<br />
It's well made, it's complex, it's vastly overpriced, and it may work very well for the right guy with the right skin chemistry. But its associations are unfortunately all bad for me - and on my skin at least it also goes far too dirty and sweaty (wrong sort of patchouli). <br />
<br />
Sorry chaps - but anyone who's telling you that this stuff is a lady magnet, is just hoarding all the womenfolk for themselves. This is a terror, not a Titan, of scent. (Just my opinion, and I guess hundreds of thousands of happy repeat customers can't be wrong ... can they? ... but I wonder how many of their male or female partners feel the same...) Also *hugely* overpriced. I'm not even going to get into how ludicrous the subculture of comparing batches is, either - a bit like a "Which of These Used Gym Bags Smells The Ripest?" competition, imho. <br />
<br />
There is no accounting for taste, but trust me: *NOT* ALL WOMEN love this smell.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="903656"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=903656#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1528157" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/560310">dmd63</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-03-22">03/22/22 08:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Smells great, but is way overrated. <br />
<br />
A true product of marketing and good publicity, nothing more. <br />
<br />
Way too expensive ($ 445/100ml!?!?!?; $ 695/250ml?!?!?!; $ 1,145/500ml?!?!?!?!) WTF?<br />
<br />
There are other great scents out there where u pay but a fraction. This stealing, pure and simple. Creed is robbing you blind.<br />
<br />
This is pure bullsh!t. No perfume, however great or good, deserves this kind of absurd prices.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="1528157"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=1528157#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent365241" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc365241" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="wesleyhclark"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/410918"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.410918.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="wesleyhclark" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Alfa-Romeo-Perfumes/Black-70093.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.70093.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Black"title="Black"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma365241ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd365241" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/410918">wesleyhclark</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2013-05-11">05/11/13 07:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Is this a joke? I mean, this IS a joke, right? <br />
<br />
I sprayed this on myself - five or six close sprays, including on my tee shirt. I got a citrus/pineapple scent at first and a nice smoky note I liked - then it was gone. In about an hour and a half. I can barely smell it on my cotton tee-shirt. <br />
<br />
No longevity, no sillage. This was from a Nordstrom sample, by the way. A premium department store selling premium scents. <br />
<br />
What is all the hype about?  <br />
<br />
My wife says it's "woodsy." She's as unimpressed as I am. <br />
<br />
$300+ a bottle? Really?</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="9828"comment_id="365241"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html?ccid=365241#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="9828" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
